            function preloadPolyfill() {
                var DOMTokenListSupports = function (tokenList, token) {
                    if (!tokenList || !tokenList.supports) {
                        return;
                    }
                    try {
                        return tokenList.supports(token);
                    }
                    catch (e) {
                        if (e instanceof TypeError) {
                            console.log("The DOMTokenList doesn't have a supported tokens list");
                        }
                        else {
                            console.error("That shouldn't have happened");
                        }
                    }
                };
                var linkSupportsPreload = DOMTokenListSupports(document.createElement('link').relList, 'preload');

                if (!linkSupportsPreload) {
                    // Dynamically load the things that relied on preload.
                    var links = document.getElementsByTagName('link');
                    for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                        var link = links[i];
                        // qualify links to those with rel=preload and as=style attrs
                        if (link.rel === 'preload' && link.getAttribute('as') === 'style' && link.dataset.fallback) {
                            // prevent re-running on link
                            link.setAttribute('rel', 'stylesheet');
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', preloadPolyfill, false);

            var analytics = window.analytics = window.analytics || [];
            if (!analytics.initialize)

                    window.console && console.error && console.error("Segment snippet included twice.");
                else {
                    analytics.invoked = !0;
                    analytics.methods = [
                        "trackSubmit", "trackClick", "trackLink", "trackForm", "pageview", "identify", "reset", "group",
                        "track", "ready", "alias", "debug", "page", "once", "off", "on"
                    ];
                    analytics.factory = function(t) {
                        return function() {
                            var e = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
                            e.unshift(t);
                            analytics.push(e);
                            return analytics;
                        }
                    };
                    for (var t = 0; t < analytics.methods.length; t++) {
                        var e = analytics.methods[t];
                        analytics[e] = analytics.factory(e);
                    }
                    analytics.load = function(t) {
                        var e = document.createElement("script");
                        e.type = "text/javascript";
                        e.async = !0;
                        e.src = ("https:" === document.location.protocol ? "https://" : "http://") +
                            "cdn.segment.com/analytics.js/v1/" +

                        initializeRudderStack();

                    analytics.ready(function() {
                        if (typeof (window.analytics.user) === "function") {
                            var user = window.analytics.user();

                            if (typeof (user) === "object") {
                                var userId = user.id();
                                var oldAnonymousId = user.anonymousId();

                                if (typeof (userId) !== "undefined" && userId !== null) {
                                    // userId is expected to be a number greater than 0. anything else should be cleared out.
                                    if (isNaN(parseInt(userId)) || parseInt(userId) <= 0) {
                                        window.analytics.reset();
                                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.track({
                                            eventInfo: {
                                                eventName: "Segment User Reset"
                                            },
                                            category: {

                            .catch(function(error) {
                                console.log(error);
                                onFinally();
                            });

                        function onFinally() {
                            if (typeof digitalData !== "undefined") {
                                attachListeners();
                            } else {
                                document.body.addEventListener("DigitalDataLoaded",
                                    function(ev) {

                                            attachListeners();
                                        }
                                    },
                                    false);
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    var handlers = {
                        page: function(pageEvent) {
                            window.analytics.page(null, pageEvent.attributes.name, pageEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                            if (window.rudderanalytics)
                                window.rudderanalytics.page(null, pageEvent.attributes.name, pageEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                        },
                        identify: function (identifyEvent) {
                            if (typeof (identifyEvent.attributes) === "object"
                                && !isNaN(parseInt(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber))
                                && parseInt(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber) > 0) {

                                if (window.rudderanalytics)

                        },

                                window.rudderanalytics.track(trackEvent.eventInfo.eventName, trackEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                        }
                    };

                    function attachListeners() {
                        // Check for missed events
                        for (var i = 0; i < window.digitalData.event.length; i++) {
                            var eventObj = window.digitalData.event[i];
                            var fn = handlers[eventObj.eventInfo.type];

                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.on("identify", handlers.identify);

                    function getGaClientId(gaAccount, tracker, timeout) {
                        return new Promise(function(resolve,  reject) {

                            var script = document.createElement("script");
                            script.type = "text/javascript";
                            script.defer = !0;
                            script.onerror = function() { return reject("Failed to load GTAG."); };
                            script.src = "https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=" + gaAccount;

                            node.parentNode.insertBefore(script, node);

                            var linkerDomains = {'domains': [""] }

                            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                            function gtag() { dataLayer.push(arguments); }
                            gtag('js', new Date());
                            gtag('config', gaAccount,
                                {
                                    'send_page_view': false,
                                    'linker': linkerDomains
                                });

                            setTimeout(function () { return reject("Timeout in getting client id."); }, timeout);

                            gtag('event', 'init_ga', {
                                 'non_interaction': true,
                                 'event_callback': function () {
                                    if (typeof window.ga !== "undefined")

                                            var trackers = window.ga.getAll();

                                                if (trackers[i].get('name').indexOf(tracker) !== -1) {
                                                    return resolve(trackers[i].get('clientId'));
                                                }
                                            }
                                            return reject("Tracker not found.");
                                        });
                                 }
                            });

                        });
                    }

                    function initializeRudderStack() {

                        var rudderanalytics = window.rudderanalytics = [];

                        var  methods = [
                            "load",
                            "page",
                            "track",
                            "identify",
                            "alias",
                            "group",
                            "ready",
                            "reset",

                            e.async = !0;

                            n.parentNode.insertBefore(e, n);
                        };
